NOTIFICATIONS   BY   GOVERNMENT
[ 1 ]
FINANCE DEPARTMENT
Secretariat, 17th August 2009
RECOMMENDATION ON  REVISION OF PENSION AND PENSIONARY BENEFITS.
No. II(1)/FIN/26(b)/2009.
[PENSION – OFFICIAL COMMITTEE ON PAY REVISION – RECOMMENDATION ON REVISION OF
PENSION AND PENSIONARY BENEFITS – ORDERS – ISSUED.]
The following Government Order is published:—
[G.O. Ms. No. 235, Finance (Pay Cell) 1st June 2009, Vaikasi 18, Thiruvalluvar Aandu 2040.]
Read:
(1) G.O.Ms.No.358, Finance (Pay Cell) Department, dated: 20—8—2008.
(2) G.O.Ms.No.496, Finance (Pay Cell) Department, dated: 17—11—2008.
(3) G.O.Ms.No.11, Finance (Pay Cell) Department, dated: 13—01—2009.
(4) G.O.Ms.No.72, Finance (Pay Cell) Department, dated: 19—02—2009.


2
Order No. 235, Finance (Pay Cell), 1st June 2009, Vaikasi 18, Thiruvalluvar Aandu-2040
The Official Committee on pay revision inter-alia has made recommendations regarding revision of
pension / family pension and pensionary benefits.
2. The Government has carefully examined the recommendations of the  Official Committee and pass
the following orders:—
(i) All the existing pensioners who retired from posts on standard pay scales and family pensioners
shall be allowed increase in pension at 40% of basic pension;
(ii) The Pension / Family Pension of the existing pre-2006 Pensioners/ Family Pensioners shall be
computed by adding the following:—
(a) The existing Pension (before commutation) / Family Pension;
(b) Dearness Pension, wherever applicable;
(c) Dearness Allowance as on 1st January 2006 i.e. @ 24% on Basic Pension / Basic Family
Pension plus dearness pension as admissible.
(d) Fitment weightage @ 40% of the existing Basic Pension (before commutation) / Basic Family
Pension.
The amount so arrived at shall be the Consolidated Pension / Family Pension with effect from
1—1—2006. The Consolidated Pension / Family Pension shall be treated as final Basic Pension with effect
from 1—1—2006 and shall be entitled for grant of Dearness Allowance sanctioned thereafter.
(iii) The revised pension / family pension arrived at as above shall be subject to a minimum pension /
family pension of Rs.3050/-per month.
(iv) The commuted portion, if any, should be deducted from the revised pension. A table indicating
revised pension / family pension under these orders from 1st January 2006 is given in Annexure-V.
(v) The upper ceiling on pension shall be 50% of the highest pay in the State Government. (The
maximum highest pay in the State Government is Rs.67000 + Grade Pay of Rs.10000/-).
(vi) The fixation of pension shall be subject to the provision that the revised pension in no case shall
be lower than fifty per cent of the minimum of the pay in the pay band plus grade pay corresponding to the
pre-revised pay scale from which the pensioner had retired. In the case of Pensioners / Family Pensioners


3
for whom pension / family pension has to be revised beneficial to them at 50% / 30% of the minimum of the
Pay + Grade Pay applicable to the post as on 1-1-2006, such of the Pensioners / Family Pensioners shall
apply to the Pension sanctioning authorities through the department they last served in the prescribed form
appended to this order. The authorities concerned shall revise both the Pension and Family Pension of the
existing pensioners.
(vii) The calculation of family pension at 30% of pay last drawn shall be followed as hitherto subject
to a minimum family pension of Rs.3050/-and the maximum family pension at 30% of the maximum of the
highest pay scale in the State Government (i.e) Rs.67000 + Grade Pay of Rs.10000/-. The existing formula
of granting enhanced family pension at fifty per cent of pay last drawn in the event of death while in service
shall be continued.
(viii) Pensioners and Family Pensioners shall be allowed dearness allowance on revised pension /
family pension as allowed to Central Government Pensioners and Family Pensioners. The new rates of
dearness allowance admissible on the revised pension / family pension shall be:
(i) With effect from 1st July 2006 : 2%
(ii) With effect from 1st January 2007 : 6%
(iii) With effect from 1st July 2007 : 9%
(iv) With effect from 1st January 2008 : 12%
(v) With effect from 1st July 2008 : 16%
(vi) With effect from 1st January 2009 : 22%
(ix) The maximum quantum of Gratuity / Death – cum -Retirement Gratuity shall be enhanced from
Rs.3.50 lakhs to Rs.10.00 lakhs.
3. The Government direct that the above benefits be granted with notional effect from 1st January 2006
and with monetary benefit from 1st January 2007.
4. The Government also direct that the existing quantum of Medical Allowance to the Pensioners / Family
Pensioners be doubled from Rs.50/-to Rs.100/-per month with effect from 1-6-2009.
5. Commutation of pension shall be permitted upto the existing rate of 33 1/3% of basic pension. These
benefits shall also be applicable to employees retiring from service on or after 1st June, 2009. For calculating
commuted value of pension the revised commutation table given in Annexure-I shall be followed.
6. Existing pensioners on 1-1-2006 whose pension is enhanced based on these orders are not entitled
to commute one third of the increase in pension. Only retirees who retired after 1-1-2006 whose pay is revised


4
due to revision of pay scale with effect from 1-1-2006 alone are entitled for commutation based on the revised
pension.
7. In the Government Order third read above, orders were issued granting Interim Arrears to the
Pensioners / Family Pensioners at the rate of three months Pension + Dearness Pension + Dearness
Allowance as on 1—1—2009 pending implementation of the recommendations of the Official Committee.
The Government direct that the arrears due to the pensioners / family pensioners be calculated for the period
from 1—1—2007 to 31—5—2009 after adjusting the interim arrears already paid and the net balance arrear
amount due shall be paid in cash in three equal annual instalments i.e. first instalment during 2009—10,
second instalment during 2010—11 and third and final instalment in 2011—12. The arrears in respect of
employees retired on or after 1—1—2006 who derive fixation of pay and consequential revision of pay,
pension and pensionary benefits upto 31—05—2009 shall also be regulated as detailed above. Illustrations
are given in Annexure-II indicating the method of arriving at the arrears and the amount to be paid to
Pensioners / Family Pensioners.
8. These orders shall apply to the following categories of pensioners:-
(i) Government pensioners, teacher pensioners of aided institutions and local bodies;
(ii) Former Travancore-Cochin State Pensioners drawing pension on 1st November 1956, in the
treasuries situated in the areas transferred to Tamil Nadu State on that date i.e. Kanyakumari District and
Shencottah Taluk of Tirunelveli District;
(iii) Pensioners drawing their pension on 1st April 1960 in the Tiruttani Sub-Treasury in whose cases
pensions were sanctioned by the Composite Madras State prior to 1st October 1953 or by the Andhra
Pradesh State prior to 1st April 1960;
(iv) Pensioners of the Ex-Governor’s Bank Establishment in receipt of ‘Mustering out’ pension;
(v) Pensioners who are in receipt of special pensions under Extraordinary Pension Rules, Madras
and Compassionate Allowance;
(vi) Ex-Pudukottai Pensioners; and
(vii) Teachers rendered surplus and whose services were terminated in the transferred areas of
Kanyakumari District and Shencottah Taluk of Tirunelveli District.
9. In the case of Pensioners / Family Pensioners specified in para 2(vi) above, they shall apply to the
authority who is competent to process and forward pension proposals to the Accountant General, Tamil Nadu
in the prescribed form (Appended to these orders). In respect of Family Pensioners, even if they are unable
to furnish all the particulars in the application form, the Pension sanctioning authorities should accept such


5
applications and process with available data. On receipt of application, in triplicate the above competent
authority shall verify the net qualifying service already certified and communicated by the Accountant
General, Tamil Nadu at the time of initial sanction of pension. He shall fix the revised pension admissible
with reference to the post held, minimum of the scale of pay and net qualifying service in the application
form itself. He shall communicate a copy of the statement duly approved to the Pension Pay Office / Treasury
Office / Sub-Treasury Office concerned with a copy to the pensioner / family pensioner. The Pension Pay
Officer/ Treasury Officer / Sub-Treasury Officer shall verify the correctness of the revised pension and make
payment as specified in paragraph-2(vi) above after making necessary entries in records maintained in his
office. In respect of pensioners drawing pension under Public Sector Bank Scheme, the concerned Bank
shall pay the revised pension as specified in paragraph-2(vi) above based on the applications received from
the departmental authorities. A ready reckoner for calculation of Pension / Family Pension with reference
to the minimum of the revised pay scale + Grade Pay is given in Annexure-IV.
10. In respect of employees whose posts were abolished and not in existence now and the concerned
pensioners / family pensioners who have requested to fix their Pension / Family Pension at the rate of 50% /
30% of the minimum of the revised Pay Band + Grade Pay, in such cases the concerned authority shall
address Finance (Pay Cell) Department directly and obtain the appropriate revised pay scale admissible
to that post(s) notionally with effect from 1-1-2006.
Regulation of Arrears in the case of employees retired between 1-1-2006 to 31-12-2008
11. For sanctioning Interim Arrears to both serving / retired employees, the crucial date of 1—1—2009
was taken into account to decide the quantum of Interim Arrears and as well as for classification of employees
viz. serving employee / pensioner. In the case of employees retired during the intervening period from
1—1—2006 to 31—12—2008, they were treated as pensioners on the crucial date of 1—1—2009 and
sanctioned three months Interim Arrears with reference to their Basic Pension / Dearness Pension / Dearness
Allowance as on 1—1—2009. As major portion is covered by service period, the arrear amount computed
on Pay Revision will be more compared to the pension revision arrears computed from 1—1—2009 to
31—5—2009. Wherever the Interim Arrears on pension could not be adjusted against pension arrears
accrued from 1—1—2009, the Pension Pay Officer/ Treasury Officer / Sub-Treasury Officer shall wait till
the revision of pension of the pensioner concerned based on the revised pay scales and take appropriate
action thereafter for adjustment of Interim Arrears.
12. The Pension Pay Officer / Treasury Officers / Sub-Treasury Officers shall work out the revised
pension / family pension and disburse the arrear amount to the Pensioners / Family Pensioners as specified
in paragraph 7 above and the copy of the above shall be marked to the Principal Accountant General who
will in turn take follow up action and verification in this regard.
13. In respect of Pensioners drawing pension under Public Sector Bank Scheme, the Commercial Banks
shall work out the revised pension and disburse the arrear amount as specified in paragraph 7 above.


6
14. The increased expenditure on account of these orders is allocable among the successor States as
per the provisions laid down under the State Re-organisation Act, 1956.
(BY ORDER OF THE GOVERNOR)
K. GNANADESIKAN,
Principal Secretary to Government.


 
7

ANNEXURE-III 
ILLUSTRATION - II

full qualifying service.  He was drawing a basic pay of Rs.8550/-  in the scale of

Band-3 is  Rs.15600—39100 with Grade pay of Rs.5400.  His pay is fixed in the 
revised scale of pay at Rs.21310.  50% of the pay last drawn is Rs.10655.  His 
pension shall be regulated as shown below:-
